## 19:59, *** 1/4. Perro Aguayo and Hiro Sito were seconds. billed as for the UWA Junior Heavyweight title, but the belt was actually Santo's UWA Welterweight title. Honaga was already IWGP Junior Heavyweight champion. Santo hurt his shoulder in the second half of the match. Perro sprayed freeze spray on Santo's shoulder and fought with Saito to distract the crowd. Santo recovered and soon did a dive. Honaga won on a low blow and a top rope elbow drop.
8) Shinjiro Otani b Great Sasuke
## 15:10, *** 3/4. Sasuke broke his foot in two plays the day before and could not walk, but managed to get thru the match anyway. Match was built around the injury.
